***honing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honing.html>honing</a> (6061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">honinch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">honey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:honing.html>honing</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hunangą</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">honey</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:honig.html>Honig</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:honing.html>honing</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>honey</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In older publications one can also encounter the word with the neutral gender.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***honk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:honk.html>honk</a> (8693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">honc</i>, likely through Old Dutch from Proto-Germanic *hank-, *hunk-. Only <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> cognates in the Frisian languages. Possibly related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haak.html>haak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hook</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoek.html>hoek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">corner</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***hoo-ha.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a> (51694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">הו־האַ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hu-ha</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a hullabaloo</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoo-has</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fuss, uproar, commotion or stir; hype; brouhaha, hullabaloo.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a big <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b> about it in the papers, and then the world completely <a href = vnd.unilang:forgot.html>forgot</a> the matter.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vagina.html>Vagina</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:linda.html>Linda</a> Howard,  <cite>Burn: A Novel</cite>, page 242:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> that make her a good judge of character, or a fool who <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> letting her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b> do her thinking for her?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Lexi Ryan,  <cite>Stilettos, Inc.</cite>, page 163:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want to lose their childish battle of wills, but neither <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> she want some parasite swimming up her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Dee Tenorio,  <cite>All Or Nothing</cite>, page 54:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">His mother <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> expressed disappointment that she'd <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> wrong, but by then, Belinda <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a butterfly on her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo-ha.html>hoo-ha</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***hooch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hooch.html>hooch</a> (29904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hoch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">high</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pdc"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooch.html>hooch</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>high</li>
<li>tall</li></ol>
<hr />

***hoodoo.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a> (45362)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently an alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:voodoo.html>voodoo</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/220px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/330px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg/440px-%C4%90avolja_Varo%C5%A1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>Some hoodoos (spires of rock).</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/220px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/330px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg/440px-Tent_rocks_between_Cavusin_and_Avanos.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4272" data-file-height="2848" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a>, showing why it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also called a <a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a> rock.</div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoodoos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A practitioner of <a href = vnd.unilang:voodoo.html>voodoo</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Supernatural bad luck, or something or someone believed to bring bad luck.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tall thin spire of rock that protrudes from the bottom of arid basins and <a href = vnd.unilang:badlands.html>badlands</a>.
<ul><li><b>2013</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philipp_Meyer" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philipp Meyer">Philipp Meyer</a>, <i>The Son</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:simon.html>Simon</a> amp; Schuster 2014, p. 71:
<dl><dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> larger than the mirage made it look—a dozen <a href = vnd.unilang:miles.html>miles</a> across and a thousand <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> deep, with <a href = vnd.unilang:fins.html>fins</a> and towers and <b>hoodoos</b> like observation <a href = vnd.unilang:posts.html>posts</a>, mesas and minor buttes, springs flowing brightly in the red rock.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">spire of rock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tent.html>tent</a> rock</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">fairy chimney</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">earth pyramid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hoodoos</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hoodooing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hoodooed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a>; to bring bad luck or misfortune to.</li></ol>

***hoofd.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a> (372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôvet</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hôoft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hōvit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*haubudą</i>. The sense “oral sex” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">head</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofden.html>hoofden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdje.html>hoofdje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>head</li>
<li>head (of an organisation), chief, boss</li>
<li>a breakwater, jetty or <a href = vnd.unilang:pier.html>pier</a> at the entrance of a sea harbour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncommon<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oral sex</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdbureau.html>hoofdbureau</a> (14446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bureau.html>bureau</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdbureau.html>hoofdbureau</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdbureau.html>hoofdbureaus</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>main office, now generally used of the main police station of a given area</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoofdbureau.html>hoofdbureau</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***hoog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a> (1127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hooch.html>hooch</a></i>, the original inflected <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hō-</i> reanalysed by analogy with the uninflected form because of word-final devoicing. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hōh</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauhaz</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hoch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">heech</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href = vnd.unilang:hag.html>hag</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">high</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">høj</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoger.html>hoger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoogst.html>hoogst</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>high
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> 887 <a href = vnd.unilang:meter.html>meter</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoge.html>hoge</a></b> <i>Mount Scenery</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogste.html>hoogste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koninkrijk.html>Koninkrijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Nederlanden.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The 887-metres-<b>high</b>  Mount Scenery <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the highest place in the Kingdom of the Netherlands.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zou.html>zou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegrepen.html>gegrepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:talen.html>talen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegelijkertijd.html>tegelijkertijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Learning three languages simultaneously would be aiming too <b>high</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoogstens.html>hoogstens</a> (9773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoogst.html>hoogst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">highest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> on the model of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">höchstens</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoogstens.html>hoogstens</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>at most</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hauhiþō</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoog.html>hoog</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hōi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hawją</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hope</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hopa</i>, from the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hopon</i> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hopen.html>hopen</a></i>). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hope</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> (228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating reassurance or confidence from the speaker:</span> certainly, surely, at all, <span class="use-with-mention">but often weak and untranslatable</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:straks.html>Straks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laat.html>laat</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genoeg.html>genoeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be late! — Nah, <b>surely</b> not, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> have plenty of time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>Wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonnetje.html>bonnetje</a>? — <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bedankt.html>bedankt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you want the receipt? — No, <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">modal particle indicating disagreement or a certain nuance with an earlier statement:</span> regardless, despite that, anyway, you know
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>kou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:valt.html>valt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a>. — <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>Nou</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The cold isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> so bad. — Well, I still think it's pretty cold <b>regardless</b>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***hoorn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a> (5582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*horn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hurną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>Hoorn</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">horn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Horn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hoarn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">horn</i>, Danish and Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">horn</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱer-</i>. Compare also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i>, from the same origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoornen.html>hoornen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorns.html>hoorns</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorntje.html>hoorntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a horn (sound device) or a <a href = vnd.unilang:bugle.html>bugle</a></li>
<li>a horn (growth projecting from the head of some animals)</li>
<li>a receiver, an earphone</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoorntje.html>hoorntje</a> (60665)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorntje.html>hoorntje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorntje.html>hoorntjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>an icecream cone</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorn.html>hoorn</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hornte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hornuta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hurznutō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱerh₂s-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hornet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hornisse</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hornet</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zitting.html>zitting</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">proceeding, meeting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in 1967.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hearing</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">proceeding for hearing arguments and discussion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>1967</b> June 9, "Zenderpark Lopik <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> IJsselmeerpolders?", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>Waarheid</a></i>, issue 157, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedeputeerde.html>Gedeputeerde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staten.html>Staten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> week in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> zgn. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoorzitting.html>hoorzitting</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partijen.html>partijen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluisterd.html>geluisterd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zullen.html>zullen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> 21 <a href = vnd.unilang:juni.html>juni</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:standpunt.html>standpunt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepalen.html>bepalen</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Provincial Executive of <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> have listened in a so-called <b>hearing</b> to both parties this week and will determine their point of view on June 21.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***hoot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> (105292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:houten.html>houten</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">huten</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hoten</i>, of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span> origin, from or related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Swedish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Swedish">Old Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-osw">huta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cast out in contempt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">hiuzen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">hūzen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to call to pursuit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>!</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">begone!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">interjection</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hui</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">huj</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:ho.html>ho</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hallo.html>hallo</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hoots</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A derisive cry or shout.</li>
<li>The cry of an owl.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A fun event or person. (See hootenanny)</li>
<li>A small particle.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1878</b>,  John Hanson Beadle,  <cite>Western <a href = vnd.unilang:wilds.html>Wilds</a>, and the <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a> who Redeem Them</cite>, Jones Brothers, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/7349592">7349592</a></small>, page 611:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Well, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Sunday morning, and the wheat nothing like ripe; but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a chance, and I got onto my <a href = vnd.unilang:reaper.html>reaper</a> and banged down every <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> of it before Monday night.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">small particle</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nearly always encountered in a negative sense in such phrases as <i>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> care a <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></i> or <i>don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> give two hoots</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derisive cry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The phrase <i>a <a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> and a <a href = vnd.unilang:holler.html>holler</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a very different meaning to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:holler.html>holler</a></i>. The former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a short distance, the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a verb of <i>derisive cry</i>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">hoots</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hooting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hooted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To cry out or shout in contempt.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1711</b>,  John Dryden,  “Satire IX”, in  <cite>Dryden’s <a href = vnd.unilang:juvenal.html>Juvenal</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Matrons and <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a> shall <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> at <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> no more,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To make the cry of an owl.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1595–1596</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Midsummer_Night%27s_Dream" class="extiw" title="w:A Midsummer Night | s Dream">A Midsommer <a href = vnd.unilang:nights.html>Nights</a> Dreame</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>,  | Act II, scene ii | :</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The clamorous owl that nightly <b>hoots</b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:wonders.html>wonders</a> / At our quaint <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To assail with contemptuous cries or shouts; to follow with derisive shouts.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1708</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Bickerstaff" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Isaac Bickerstaff">Isaac Bickerstaff</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:jonathan.html>Jonathan</a> Swift],  <cite>Predictions for the Year 1708</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://jonathanswiftarchive.org.uk/search/text_4_3_2.html?page=d2e215">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And I will be content, that Partridge, and the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of his Clan, may <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hoot.html>hoot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> for a Cheat and Impostor, if I fail in any single Particular of <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>Moment</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To sound the horn of a vehicle</li></ol>
</body>

***hop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> hop (5676)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
